            window.headerScripts.cacheBuster = function() {
                let cacheBuster = "";
                if (window.location.href.indexOf("1.") !== -1) {
                    cacheBuster = "?login=true";
                    if (window.location.href.indexOf("?") !== -1) {
                        cacheBuster = "&login=true";
                    }
                }

                return cacheBuster;
            }

  <script>
   adformScripts.setupTakeover = function(advertData, takeoverFrequencyResetTimer){
    let takeoverCookie = headerScripts.getCookie('takeover_cookie');
    if( takeoverCookie == "" ){
        let mId = adformScripts.defineTag('ad-takeover', advertData);
        window.adformQueue = window.adformQueue || [];
        window.adformQueue.push(function(){
            adformtag.onLoaded(mId, function (adItem){
                if(!adItem.isEmpty){
                    document.getElementById('ad-takeover').style.display = "initial";
                    headerScripts.createCookie('takeover_cookie', 'tkvr_ckvl', takeoverFrequencyResetTimer * 60);
                }else{
                    document.getElementById('ad-takeover').remove()
                    return;
                }
            });
        });
    }else{
        document.getElementById('ad-takeover').remove()
        return;
    }
};
  </script>

  <script>
   (function (headerScripts) {

	var hasNoProductsCookie = 'no_products';
	let nextButton;
	var sharesLeft = 0;
	var mainColumn;
	var modalElement;
	var firstBoughtProductId;
	var errorElement;


	function init() {
		firstBoughtProductId = getFirstBoughtProductId();

		if (firstBoughtProductId !== '') {
			mainColumn = document.getElementById('mainColumnOnboarding');
			modalElement = document.querySelector('.c-modal-onboarding');

			openModalAndSetup();
		}
	}


	function openModalAndSetup() {
		window.modal.openModal(modalElement.closest('.js-modal-viewport'));

		window.slm.stepsTotal = 1;

		if (!window.isApp) {
			window.slm.stepsTotal++;
		}

		if (location.hostname.indexOf('gp.se') > -1) {
			var productsObj = headerScripts.getUserData().active_products;

			if (typeof productsObj !== 'undefined') {
				var products = productsObj.join();
				var hasAtLeastEgp = products.indexOf('digital_tidning') > -1 || products.indexOf('e_gp') > -1 || products
				.indexOf('gp_e_gp') > -1;

				if (hasAtLeastEgp) {
					window.slm.stepsTotal++;
				}
			}
		}

		fetch('/internal-api/familysharing', {
			method: 'GET',
			credentials: 'same-origin',
		}).then(function(response) {
			return response.json();
		}).then(function(json) {
			if (typeof json.data !== 'undefined') {
				if (typeof json.data[0] !== 'undefined') {
					sharesLeft = json.data[0].sharingLimit;
					firstBoughtProductId = json.data[0].productId;
				} else {
					sharesLeft = 0;
				}

				if (sharesLeft > 0) {
					window.slm.stepsTotal++;
				}
			}

			renderFirstViewFollow();
		}).catch(function(e) {
			console.error(e);
		});
	}


	function renderFirstViewFollow() {

		window.slm.currentStep = 1;
		renderTemplate('onboardingTemplate');

		checkFollowButtons();

		headerScripts.pushPageview('/onboarding/folj-tagg', 'Onboarding - följ tagg');

		addFollowButtonClickListeners();

		if (window.innerWidth < 800) {
			makeSlider();
		}

		var userTagsTitles = document.querySelectorAll('.c-user-tags__title');

		if (userTagsTitles.length > 1) {
			var maxHeight = Math.max(userTagsTitles[0].offsetHeight, userTagsTitles[1].offsetHeight) + 'px';

			userTagsTitles[0].style.height = maxHeight;
			userTagsTitles[1].style.height = maxHeight;
		}

		headerScripts.eraseCookie(hasNoProductsCookie);

		if (nextButton !== null) {
			nextButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
				if (sharesLeft > 0) {
					renderViewShare(sharesLeft, firstBoughtProductId);
				} else {
					renderViewAppInfo();
				}
			});
		}
	}


	function renderViewShare(sharesLeft, productId) {
		renderTemplate('onboardingTemplateShare');

		headerScripts.pushPageview('/onboarding/familjedelning', 'Onboarding - familjedelning');

		var shareButton = document.querySelector('.js-onboarding-sharing__trigger');
		var elementEmail = document.querySelector('.c-onboarding--share-email');
		errorElement = document.querySelector('.c-onboarding-sharing__error');


		document.querySelector('.sharesLeft').innerText = getShareText(sharesLeft);
		document.querySelector('.sharesLeftMinusOne').innerText = getShareText(sharesLeft - 1);

		elementEmail.addEventListener('focus', function () {
			errorElement.innerText = '';
		});

		shareButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
			handleShareClick(elementEmail, productId);
		});

		if (!window.isApp) {
			nextButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
				renderViewAppInfo();
			});
		} else {
			if (nextButton !== null) {
				nextButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
					renderViewCrossword();
				});
			}
		}
	}

	function getShareText(sharesLeft) {
		var shareText = '';

		if (sharesLeft === 0) {
			shareText = 'inga delningar';
		} else if (sharesLeft === 1) {
			shareText = '1 delning';
		} else {
			shareText = sharesLeft + ' delningar';
		}

		return shareText;
	}

	function handleShareClick(elementEmail, productId) {
		var output = '';

		if (!siteScripts.shareSubscription.validateEmail(elementEmail.value)) {
			output = 'Du har inte angivit en giltlig e-postadress';
		} else {
			output = siteScripts.shareSubscription.callSharingApi(productId, elementEmail.value);
		}

		if (output !== '') {
			errorElement.innerHTML = output;
		} else {
			document.querySelector('.c-user-sharing__form').classList.add('u-hidden');
			document.querySelector('.c-user-sharing__pending-wrapper').classList.remove('u-hidden');
			document.querySelector('.c-user-sharing__item__name').innerText = elementEmail.value;
			document.querySelector('.c-onboarding-sharing__intro--shared').classList.add('u-hidden');

			var eventInfo = {
				category: 'account',
				action: 'share account'
			};

			headerScripts.pushEvent(
				'share account',
				eventInfo
			);
		}
	}


	function checkFollowButtons() {
		var buttonText = ["Följ", "Följer"];

		var followData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("followData"));

		function setFollowButtonStatus(follow, actionLink) {
			if (actionLink != null) {
				var btn = actionLink.querySelector('button.c-btn--follow');
				if (btn != null) {
					var parent = btn.closest('.myPagesTagAction');
					var textAddon = "";
					var btnPushNoticeLink = jQuery(parent).prev();
					var btnPushNoticeButton = btnPushNoticeLink.find('button').first();

					if (follow) {
						actionLink.classList.add('following');
						btn.innerHTML = buttonText[1] + textAddon;
						btnPushNoticeButton.removeAttr('disabled');
					} else {
						actionLink.classList.remove('following');
						btn.innerHTML = buttonText[0] + textAddon;
						btnPushNoticeButton.attr('disabled', 'disabled');
					}
				}
			}
		}

			function isFollowing(name) {
			if (followData != null && name != null) {
				return JSON.stringify(followData).indexOf(name) > -1;
			}
			return false;
		}


		document.querySelectorAll('.myPagesTagAction').forEach(function (item) {
			var name = item.getAttribute('data-tagname');
			setFollowButtonStatus(isFollowing(name), item);
			if (item.className.indexOf('c-user-tags__list__item-notice') === -1) {
				item.style.display = 'inline-block';
			}
		});
	}


	function renderViewAppInfo() {
		renderTemplate('onboardingAppTemplate');

		var eventInfo = {
			category: 'engagement',
			action: 'download',
			label: ''
		};

		headerScripts.pushPageview('/onboarding/nedladdning-app', 'Onboarding - nedladdning app');

		document.querySelector('.onboarding__app_ios').addEventListener('click', function () {

			eventInfo.label = 'apple';

			headerScripts.pushEvent(
				'download',
				eventInfo
			);

		});

		document.querySelector('.onboarding__app_android').addEventListener('click', function () {

			eventInfo.label = 'google';

			headerScripts.pushEvent(
				'download',
				eventInfo
			);

		});

		if (nextButton !== null) {
			nextButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
				renderViewCrossword();
			});
		}
	}


	function renderViewCrossword() {
		renderTemplate('onboardingCrosswordTemplate');

		headerScripts.pushPageview('/onboarding/korsord', 'Onboarding - korsord');

		document.querySelector('.js-onboarding--crossword').addEventListener('click', function () {
			location.href = '/korsord?linkAttribution=onboarding';
		});
	}


	function addFollowButtonClickListeners() {
		var followButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.myPagesTagAction');

		if (followButtons === null) {
			return; // EXIT
		}

		followButtons.forEach(function (button) {
			button.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
				var buttonClicked = event.target;

				if (buttonClicked.className.indexOf('following') > -1) {
					return; // EXIT if unfollowing
				}

				sendFollowEvent(buttonClicked.dataset.tagname);

				return false;
			});
		});
	}


	function makeSlider() {

		var flexWrapper = document.querySelector('.c-modal-onboarding');

		flexWrapper.classList.add('is-slider');

		new Glide(".glide-onboarding", {
			type: 'slider',
			swipeThreshold: 20,
			perView: 1,
			gap: 30,
			peek: {
				before: 0,
				after: 50
			}
		}).mount();
	}

	function renderTemplate(template) {
		mainColumn.innerHTML = '';
		var templateNode = getTemplate(template);
		mainColumn.classList = '';
		mainColumn.classList.add(template);
		mainColumn.appendChild(templateNode);


		if (headerScripts.checkDevice().text === 'Mobile') {
			modalElement.querySelector('.c-modal__body').scrollTo(0, 0);
		}

		renderFooter();

		window.slm.currentStep = window.slm.currentStep + 1;

		nextButton = mainColumn.querySelector('.js-onboarding-next');

		const closeButton = mainColumn.querySelector('.js-close-modal');

		if (closeButton !== null) {
			closeButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
				modal.closeModal(modalElement);
			});
		}
	}


	function renderFooter() {
		var footer = '';

		if (window.slm.currentStep === window.slm.stepsTotal) {
			footer = '<button class="c-btn c-btn--small c-btn--round c-btn--onboarding c-btn--onboarding-last js-close-modal">Stäng</button>';
		} else {
			footer = '<button class="c-btn c-btn--small c-btn--round c-btn--onboarding js-onboarding-app c-btn--onboarding--app js-onboarding-next">Gå vidare</button>';
		}

		footer = footer + '<div class="c-onboarding__pages"> <span class="c-onboarding__current-page">Steg ' + window.slm.currentStep + '</span> av ' + window.slm.stepsTotal + '</div>';

		var footerElement = mainColumn.querySelector('.c-onboarding__footer');

		footerElement.innerHTML = footerElement.innerHTML + footer;
	}


	function getTemplate(templateName) {

		let templateElement = document.getElementById(templateName);

		if (templateElement === null) {
			return null;
		}

		return document.importNode(templateElement.content, true);
	}


	function getFirstBoughtProductId() {

		var userData = headerScripts.getUserData();
		const currentActiveProducts = userData.active_products;
		let currentActiveProductsNr = 0;
		var productId = '';

		if (typeof currentActiveProducts !== 'undefined') {
			currentActiveProductsNr = currentActiveProducts.length;
			hasNoProductsCookie = hasNoProductsCookie + userData.paywayId;

			if (currentActiveProductsNr === 0) {
				headerScripts.createCookie(hasNoProductsCookie, true, 60 * 60); // 1 timme
			} else {
				if (headerScripts.readCookie(hasNoProductsCookie)) {
					productId = currentActiveProducts[0];
				}
			}
		}

		return productId;
	}


	function sendFollowEvent(tagname) {

		var eventInfo = {
			category: 'engagement',
			action: 'follow',
			label: tagname
		};

		headerScripts.pushEvent(
			'follow',
			eventInfo
		);
	}

	function sendAppEvent() {

		var eventInfo = {
			category: 'engagement',
			action: 'follow',
			label: tagname
		};

		headerScripts.pushEvent(
			'follow',
			eventInfo
		);
	}


	headerScripts.onboarding = {
		hasNoProductsCookie: hasNoProductsCookie,
		init: init,
		openModalAndSetup: openModalAndSetup,
		renderFirstViewFollow: renderFirstViewFollow,
		renderViewShare: renderViewShare,
		getShareText: getShareText,
		handleShareClick: handleShareClick,
		checkFollowButtons: checkFollowButtons,
		renderViewAppInfo: renderViewAppInfo,
		renderViewCrossword: renderViewCrossword,
		addFollowButtonClickListeners: addFollowButtonClickListeners,
		makeSlider: makeSlider,
		renderTemplate: renderTemplate,
		renderFooter: renderFooter,
		getTemplate: getTemplate,
		getFirstBoughtProductId: getFirstBoughtProductId,
		sendFollowEvent: sendFollowEvent,
		sendAppEvent: sendAppEvent
	}

})(window.headerScripts = window.headerScripts || { });
  </script>

  <script>
   var adformtag = adformtag || [];
        var adformQueue = adformQueue || [];

        /** Set global targeting for adform */
        var loggedIn = headerScripts.isLoggedIn();
        var departmentPath = ["start"];
        adformtag.push(function() {
            adformtag.setGlobalTargeting('logged_in', loggedIn);
            for(var i = 0; i < departmentPath.length; ++i) {
                adformtag.setGlobalTargeting('category', window.encodeURIComponent(departmentPath[i]));
            }
        });
        /* Figure out lwKeywords from departmentPath using configured mapping values. */
        var lwKeywordsMap = JSON.parse('[[\"start\",\"start\"],[\"nyheter\",\"nyheter\"],[\"sport\",\"sport\"],[\"ekonomi\",\"ekonomi\"],[\"kultur-noje\",\"kultur-noje\"],[\"familj\",\"familj\"],[\"opinion\",\"opinion\"],[\"bostad\",\"bostad\"],[\"tv\",\"tv\"]]');
        window.slm.lwKeywords = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < lwKeywordsMap.length; i++) {
            if (departmentPath.indexOf(lwKeywordsMap[i][0]) !== -1) {
                window.slm.lwKeywords = [lwKeywordsMap[i][1]];

  <script>
   // IE Object.assign FIX. IE 11 does not support Object.assign
    if (typeof Object.assign != 'function') {
      Object.assign = function(target, varArgs) { // .length of function is 2
        'use strict';
        if (target == null) { // TypeError if undefined or null
          throw new TypeError('Cannot convert undefined or null to object');
        }

        var to = Object(target);

        for (var index = 1; index < arguments.length; index++) {
          var nextSource = arguments[index];

          if (nextSource != null) { // Skip over if undefined or null
            for (var nextKey in nextSource) {
              // Avoid bugs when hasOwnProperty is shadowed
              if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(nextSource, nextKey)) {
                to[nextKey] = nextSource[nextKey];
              }
            }
          }
        }
        return to;
      };
    }
  </script>

     <script>
      document.querySelectorAll('.triggerToggle').forEach(function(toggleElement) {

          toggleElement.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
            var _this = this;
            var clickedNode = event.target.nodeName;

            if (clickedNode === 'A' || clickedNode === 'SPAN' || (clickedNode === 'LI' && !event.target.classList.contains('triggerToggle'))) {
              return; // EXIT
            }

            event.preventDefault();
            event.stopPropagation();

            var toggleClassName = 'c-nav-dropdown--open';
            var subPages = this.parentElement.querySelectorAll('li');

            subPages.forEach(function(element) {
              if (element === _this) {
                if (_this.classList.contains(toggleClassName)) {
                  _this.classList.remove(toggleClassName);
                } else {
                  _this.classList.add(toggleClassName);
                }
              } else {
                element.classList.remove(toggleClassName);
              }
            });

          });
        });
     </script>

      <!-- MARVAN 2020-07-10: Flowplayer fullscreen fix Safari -->
      <script>
       ;(function(){
  if (false === /^((?!chrome|android).)*safari/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
    return; // Only run for Safari?
  }
  function fixVideo(article) {
    var embeds = article.querySelectorAll('script[src*="//cdn.flowplayer.com/players/"]');
    for (var i = 0; i < embeds.length; i++) {
      var parent = embeds[i].parentNode;
      var backup = parent.style.backgroundImage;
      parent.removeAttribute('style');
      parent.style.backgroundImage = backup;
    }
  }
  var config = { attributes: false, childList: true, subtree: false };
  var observer = new MutationObserver(function(actions){
    fixVideo(actions[0].target);
  });
  var articles = document.querySelectorAll('article.c-article');
  for (var i = 0; i < articles.length; i++) {
    if (articles[i].children.length === 0) {
      observer.observe(articles[i], config);
    } else {
      fixVideo(articles[i]);
    }
  }
})();
      </script>
      <script>
       (function(siteScripts){

function getNotificationsBadgeNumber(){

return jQuery.ajax({
type: 'POST',
url : '/internal-api/user/notificationsnumber', 
data: JSON.stringify({data: getFollowDataTagNames()}),
dataType: 'JSON',
headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
credentials: 'same-origin',
success: function(response) {
//return response.count > 0;
return response;
}
});

function getFollowDataTagNames() {
var namesList = '';

var followDataJson = localStorage.getItem("followData");
if (followDataJson != null) {
var obj = JSON.parse(followDataJson);
Object.keys(obj).forEach(function(key, index) {
var follow = obj[key][0];
if (follow) {
if (index === 0) {
namesList += key;
} else {
namesList += ',' + key;
}
}
});	
}

return namesList;
}
}

siteScripts.getNotificationsBadgeNumber = getNotificationsBadgeNumber;

})(window.siteScripts = window.siteScripts || {});
      </script>
